 The ramjanmabhoomi-babri Masjid dispute in the Supreme Court was also heard on the 19th day on Wednesday
 sarvocch adaalat main sunni vakf board ke vakil rajeev dhawan ne apni daleelein pesh kin
 He started his arguments from Tuesday which continued on Wednesday
 buudhvaar ko sunwaayee ke apadet:04
 02 PM: He said, there is talk of Babur coming to Ayodhya in 1528 and building a mosque
 shilaon par likhe aalekh par koi shaq o shubahaa nahin kiya ja saktaa
 It is recorded in the Gazetteer that there was a mosque near the birthplace where the Nirmohi Akhara built the platform
 1825 ke aasapaas vahaan singhdwar banane kii ijaajat par bhi hangaamaa hua tha
 Then the court ordered to maintain the status quo i
e
 worship inside the mosque
 04
 00 PM: Dhawan reading various documents said, sketches and descriptions of historical Carnegie also speak of Babur's mosque
 kasuti khambhe buddha math kaa hissaa hone kaa anumaan lagaaya gaya tha
 The Hindus had tried to occupy the disputed building thrice
 03
 57 PM: Dhawan said, in the 1828 Gazetteer, Hemleton made no mention of the mosque
 jabaki marco polo ne to zikr kiya he
 It was claimed that 360 temples were demolished
 east india company ke gajetir main bhi kaha gaya ki vahaan masjid thi, jise babar kaa banaaya hua kaha jaataa he or vahiin hindu ram kaa janmasthan maanate hai
 03
 40 pm:rajeev dhawan ne kaha ki agar yachika samay se daakhil nahin hui to iskaa matlab ye nahin ki vahaan masjid nahin thi
 The mosque does not cease to exist by placing idols
 naa hi lagaataar namaaj naa padhane se masjid ke vajood par sawaal khadey ho sakate hai
 The Nirmohi Akhara too has not claimed internal enclosures many times
 03
 32 PM: Sunni Waqf Board lawyer Rajeev Dhawan said in the Supreme Court that even then judgments are clear that Muslims used to worship inside the building and outside the Hindu compound
 baahar chabutare par pathar par bani charan padukaayen bhi bani thim, mahant raghubar das kii apil tab kii sthaneey court ne khaarij bhi kar di thi
 Dhawan said that the Nirmohi Arena had gone to Ramghat, once the disputed building needed repairing, the administration had taken the plunge from the Muslims
 tab ram chabutara hi ram janmasthan mana jaataa tha
 Dhawan read portions of Trafan Thaler's book citing the written argument of Nirmohi Akhara
 vakil ne kaha ki tab aisi manyata thi ki ram chabutare vaali jagah par paidaa hue the, ye jagah bahari ahaate main he
 Rajiv Dhawan said that Ram Chabutara was also called the altar
 itihaas main nirmohi akhaade ke kai kadam or kai aadesh ye sabit karte hai ki masjid thi or tab ke mahant raghubar das ne sirf ram chabutare par ramalala kii seva puja karne kaa anurodh kiya tha
 The lawyer said that the stand of the Akhara and the orders of the administration dismantle the Nirmohi Akhara's claim that there was no mosque there
 12
 15 PM: Meanwhile, Rajiv Dhawan attacked the Nirmohi Arena and said that the Nirmohi Arena has claimed the inner courtyard, not the outer court
 nirmohi akhaada sirf sarkaar ke khilaaf tha
 In such a situation, how can you claim now? Further Justice DY Chandrachud said that if you accept the right of worship to the arena, then it means that you are assuming that there were idols there
 aise main ye hissaa saamne nahin aata he jisapar aap masjid kaa daawa karte hai
 Dhawan said that the right to worship was given on the basis of ease
 nirmohi akhaada ko sirf puja kaa adhikaar diya gaya, aise main jameen uski nahin hoti he
 12
 00 pm:supreme court main vakil rajeev dhawan ne kaha ki 1885 main nirmohi akhaada ne puja kaa adhikaar maanga, jiske baad unhen chabutara diya gaya
 Then there was no issue of title suit
 iske baad justise chandrachud ne kaha ki devtaa kaa adhikaar sahajata se taalluk rakhata he
 The suit was filed in 1885, but the title suit was not claimed
 jaj ne kaha ki hamen aaj ke muslim kanoon ke mutabik aage badhanaa hoga
 Further, Justice Bhushan said that you are saying that only the rule of Quran will not apply to the mosque
 justise chandrachud ne kaha ki aapkaa maamla aapasi sashastitv kaa he
 However, Rajiv Dhawan said that my case is of Waqf
 or ye hamaari property he
 Some people will come and say that they are worshiping here, we cannot stop them
 11
 50 AM: After the decision of Justice Khan, Justice Sharma in the Supreme Court, now Rajiv Dhawan is discussing the comments of Justice Agarwal, the head of the Bench
 unhone kaha ki bahari ahaate se murtiyon ko gumbad ke neeche rakhaa gaya or ek kahani garh lee gai
 11
 30 am:buudhvaar ko sunwaayee ke dauraan muslim pakshakaar kii taraf se kaha gaya ki bahari ahaata to shuru se nirmohi akhaade ke kabje main rahaa he, ab kyon elahabaad hoicourt ke aadhaar par daleelein di ja rahi hai
 The quarrel is over the inner enclosure, which was forcibly captured
 rajeev dhawan ne adaalat main kaha ki jis dhaanche ko todaa gaya, vahaan pehle mandir hone ke pukhta saboot nahin mili the
 There is now a dispute about the adversity position
 hoicourt ke faisle ke hawaale se rajeev dhawan ne kaha ki bich vaale gumbad ke neeche jabaran ramalala kii murti rakhkar vivaad khadaa kiya gaya

 aapako bataa den ki supreme court main is masale kii sunwaayee 6 agast se rojaanaa chal rahi he
 Till now the lawyers of Nirmohi Akhara, Ramlala, Hindu Mahasabha have submitted their arguments
 railway steshnon ko vishwastareey banane ke liye railway puri tarah se prayaas kar rahi he
 In this series, the government company Infrastructure Consultancy Rights (RITES) Limited will now give its advice for projects to be made for modernization of railway stations
 ritis ne iske liye bhartiya rail khanpan evam paryaton nigam (iarsitisi) ke saath ek samjhaute par hastakshar kiye hai
 IRCTC signed a Memorandum of Understanding (mou) with RITES (RITES), under which RITES will undertake the design and engineering for projects apart from managing the bidding process for selection of construction agencies
 bhartiya rail kaa ek mini ratna kahe jane vaali company iarsitisi ucch gunvattta vaale khanpan, paryaton or tikat seva pradaan karne se lekar yatriyon ke liye infrastracchar or suvidhaon main sudhaar karne ke liye apane kaary kshetra kaa vistaar kar rahi he
 Recently Indian Railways has decided to entrust the management of its Retiring Room and Bedroom to IRCTC for better utilization of existing infrastructure
 iarsitisi in suvidhaon ko charanbaddh tareeke se puraa karne, unki marammat or navinikaran karne or unhen yatriyon ke liye uplabdh karaane ke liye khud ko taiyaar kar rahaa he
 Under the Memorandum of Understanding, IRCTC will hand over all the works including planning, design, tendering, construction and supervision, inspection and commission to the rights as per requirement, for works and allied facilities at the railway station, on a project by project basis

 ) mumbai main varsova police ne bhartiya janata yuva morcha ke purv adhyaksh ganesh pandeya ke khilaaf chhedhkhani kaa maamla darj kar liya he

 ipisi kii dhara 354(a), 509, 34 ke tahat darj maamle main ganesh pandeya ke saath unke saathiyon ko bhi aaropee banaaya gaya he
 On the complaint of the victim who is also a member of the Bharatiya Janata Party, the party has already expelled Ganesh Pandey from the party
 peedita ne police ko bataaya he ki vah saal 2003 se bijepi kii sadsy he
 On March 3, 2016, about 183 members of the Bharatiya Janata Yuva Morcha had gone from Garib Rath to participate in the executive meeting held in Mathura
 raste main ganesh pandey ne ashleel baton se use apamaanit kiya
 But even after being insulted she did not resist anything and slept quietly on her berth
 ganesh pandeya ne aawaaj dekar use uthaane kii koshish kii, lekin usne koi jawaab nahin diya tab ganesh ne berth ke neeche hi mobile par porn film play kiya, jisaki aawaaj duusare yatri bhi sun rahe the
 According to the victim, all people stayed at the Brij Bhumi Hotel in Mathura on 4 March
 peedita hotel ke room number 208 main party kii ek duusari mahila kaaryakarta ke saath rukii thi
 In the night, while she was rehearsing the dance in the hotel corridor, the youth front officer Himanshu Padwal was repeatedly saying that Ganesh Pandey was calling
 lekin wo nahin gai, kyunki use pataa tha ki vahaan wo log sharaab pi rahe the
 At the end of rehearsal at about one and a half, she went to her room
 lekin tabhi himanshu padaval or amit shellar uske manaa karne ke baad bhi jabaran use room number 204 main le gaye
 There were many other officials in the room including Ganesh Pandey
 kuch mahila padaadhikari bhi maujuud thim
 The comments ganesh pandeya ke saath kuch log sharaab pi rahe the
 Everyone started laughing as they went to the victim's room
 ganesh ne gande or ashleel chutkule sunaane shuru kiye
 The victim's virginity was also questioned
 naaraaz hokar jab wo jane lagi tab ganesh pandeya ne peechha kiya or donon haath pakadakar rokane kii koshish kii
 With her free hand she went to the room with her fellow worker and closed the door from inside
 pandeya or unke saathiyon ne tab jor-jor se darwaja peeta or kholane ko kaha
 On not opening the door, she started playing porn films with Phool Volume on mobile
 pandeya or unke doston ke us harakat se peedita ke saath duusari mahila kaaryakarta bhi ghabara gai thi
 According to the victim, all returned to Mumbai on 7 March
 19 march ko bijepi ke padaadhikariyon ke saath milakar ganesh pandey kii shikaayat kii
 On March 22, at the state party office, he made a written complaint to Mumbai BJP President Ashish Shelar
 jiske baad party ne ganesh pandeya ko nikaal diya
 Ganesh Pandey, on the other hand, termed the charge against him as a conspiracy to defame him
 peedita jo khud bhi bhartiya janata party kii sadasya he, uski shikaayat par party pehle hi ganesh pandeya ko party se nishkashit kar chuki he
 The victim has told the police that she is a member of the BJP since the year 2003
 3 march 2016 ko bhartiya janata yuva morcha ke taqariban 183 sadsy mathura main yojit kaaryakarini main hissaa lene garib rath se gaye the
 On the way, Ganesh Pandey humiliated him with vulgar things
 lekin apmaan sahakar bhi usne tab kuch virodh nahin kiya or chupchaap apane berth par so gai

 peedita ke mutabik 4 march ko mathura ke brij bhoomi hotel main sabhi log tehre the

 tippaniyan Some people were drinking alcohol with Ganesh Pandey
 peedita ke kamare main jate hi sabhi hansane lage

 peedita ke comarya par bhi sawaal uthaaya

 1
 Do not delay even on the first day of office

 3

 1
 Disorientation from Basic Principles The biggest reason for disenchantment of voters with Congress is believed to be the deviation from its core principles
 garibon-kisaanon kii baat karne vaali party par corporate culture haaavee ho gaya

 nateeja in virgon kii nai or swatantra leadership taiyaar hui

 3

 4

 tippaniyan Khurshid said, "he will be remembered as a man with whom India was comfortable

 court ne us yachikakarta ko bhi notice jari kiya he, jisaki yachika par hoicourt ne faisla sunaaya tha
 The court wondered how the Noida Authority allowed the construction of the 40-floor building and if these buildings were to be demolished, the Authority would have to bear the brunt
 court ne kaha ki yadi in imaaraton ko giraaya gaya to praadhikaran ko hi in flats maalikon ko dhan kaa bhugtan karnaa hoga, kyonki usee kii mileebhagat se in imaaraton ko manjuuri di gai thi
 The court also questioned how 40 floors were constructed from 24th floor during construction
